\DoxyCodeLine{490 }
\DoxyCodeLine{491 \textcolor{comment}{// A 24 byte string class (can be as small as 17 for x64 and 13 for x86) that can hold strings with length}}
\DoxyCodeLine{492 \textcolor{comment}{// of up to 23 chars on the stack before going on the heap -\/ the last byte of the buffer is used for:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{493 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ "{}is small"{} bit -\/ the highest bit -\/ if "{}0"{} then it is small -\/ otherwise its "{}1"{} (128)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{494 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ if small -\/ capacity left before going on the heap -\/ using the lowest 5 bits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{495 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ if small -\/ 2 bits are left unused -\/ the second and third highest ones}}
\DoxyCodeLine{496 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ if small -\/ acts as a null terminator if strlen() is 23 (24 including the null terminator)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{497 \textcolor{comment}{//              and the "{}is small"{} bit remains "{}0"{} ("{}as well as the capacity left"{}) so its OK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{498 \textcolor{comment}{// Idea taken from this lecture about the string implementation of facebook/folly -\/ fbstring}}
\DoxyCodeLine{499 \textcolor{comment}{// https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=kPR8h4-\/qZdk}}
\DoxyCodeLine{500 \textcolor{comment}{// TODO:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{501 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ optimizations -\/ like not deleting memory unnecessarily in operator= and etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{502 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ resize/reserve/clear}}
\DoxyCodeLine{503 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ substr}}
\DoxyCodeLine{504 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ replace}}
\DoxyCodeLine{505 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ back/front}}
\DoxyCodeLine{506 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ iterator stuff}}
\DoxyCodeLine{507 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ find \& friends}}
\DoxyCodeLine{508 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ push\_back/pop\_back}}
\DoxyCodeLine{509 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ assign/insert/erase}}
\DoxyCodeLine{510 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ relational operators as free functions -\/ taking const char* as one of the params}}
\DoxyCodeLine{511     \textcolor{keyword}{class }DOCTEST\_INTERFACE \mbox{\hyperlink{classdoctest_1_1_string}{String}}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1175 \textcolor{comment}{// This will check if there is any way it could find a operator like member or friend and uses it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1176 \textcolor{comment}{// If not it doesn't find the operator or if the operator at global scope is defined after}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1177 \textcolor{comment}{// this template, the template won't be instantiated due to SFINAE. Once the template is not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1178 \textcolor{comment}{// instantiated it can look for global operator using normal conversions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1179 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define SFINAE\_OP(ret,op) decltype((void)(doctest::detail::declval<L>() op doctest::detail::declval<R>()),ret\{\})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1180 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1181 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DOCTEST\_DO\_BINARY\_EXPRESSION\_COMPARISON(op, op\_str, op\_macro)                              \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1182 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    template <typename R>                                                                          \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1183 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    DOCTEST\_NOINLINE SFINAE\_OP(Result,op) operator op(const R\&\& rhs) \{                             \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1184 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    bool res = op\_macro(doctest::detail::forward<const L>(lhs), doctest::detail::forward<const R>(rhs));                                                             \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1185 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        if(m\_at \& assertType::is\_false)                                                            \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1186 \textcolor{preprocessor}{            res = !res;                                                                            \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1187 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        if(!res || doctest::getContextOptions()-\/>success)                                          \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1188 \textcolor{preprocessor}{            return Result(res, stringifyBinaryExpr(lhs, op\_str, rhs));                             \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1189 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        return Result(res);                                                                        \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1190 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \}                                                                                              \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1191 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    template <typename R ,typename enable\_if<!doctest::detail::is\_rvalue\_reference<R>::value, void >::type* = nullptr> \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1192 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    DOCTEST\_NOINLINE SFINAE\_OP(Result,op) operator op(const R\& rhs) \{                              \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1193 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    bool res = op\_macro(doctest::detail::forward<const L>(lhs), rhs);                              \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1194 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        if(m\_at \& assertType::is\_false)                                                            \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1195 \textcolor{preprocessor}{            res = !res;                                                                            \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1196 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        if(!res || doctest::getContextOptions()-\/>success)                                          \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1197 \textcolor{preprocessor}{            return Result(res, stringifyBinaryExpr(lhs, op\_str, rhs));                             \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1198 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        return Result(res);                                                                        \(\backslash\)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3240 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3241 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3242     \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{3243     \textcolor{keyword}{using }AtomicOrMultiLaneAtomic = std::atomic<T>;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3244 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else }\textcolor{comment}{// DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3245     \textcolor{comment}{// Provides a multilane implementation of an atomic variable that supports add, sub, load,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3246     \textcolor{comment}{// store. Instead of using a single atomic variable, this splits up into multiple ones,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3247     \textcolor{comment}{// each sitting on a separate cache line. The goal is to provide a speedup when most}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3248     \textcolor{comment}{// operations are modifying. It achieves this with two properties:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3249     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3250     \textcolor{comment}{// * Multiple atomics are used, so chance of congestion from the same atomic is reduced.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3251     \textcolor{comment}{// * Each atomic sits on a separate cache line, so false sharing is reduced.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3252     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3253     \textcolor{comment}{// The disadvantage is that there is a small overhead due to the use of TLS, and load/store}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3254     \textcolor{comment}{// is slower because all atomics have to be accessed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3255     \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{3256     \textcolor{keyword}{class }MultiLaneAtomic}
\DoxyCodeLine{3257     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3258         \textcolor{keyword}{struct }CacheLineAlignedAtomic}
\DoxyCodeLine{3259         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3260             std::atomic<T> atomic\{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3261             \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} padding[DOCTEST\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS\_CACHE\_LINE\_SIZE -\/ \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(std::atomic<T>)];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3262         \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3263         CacheLineAlignedAtomic m\_atomics[DOCTEST\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS\_THREAD\_LANES];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3264 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3265         \textcolor{keyword}{static\_assert}(\textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(CacheLineAlignedAtomic) == DOCTEST\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS\_CACHE\_LINE\_SIZE,}
\DoxyCodeLine{3266                       \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}guarantee one atomic takes exactly one cache line"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{3267 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3268     \textcolor{keyword}{public}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3269         T operator++() DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} fetch\_add(1) + 1; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3270 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3271         T operator++(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int}) DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} fetch\_add(1); \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3272 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3273         T fetch\_add(T arg, std::memory\_order order = std::memory\_order\_seq\_cst) DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3274             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} myAtomic().fetch\_add(arg, order);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3275         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3276 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3277         T fetch\_sub(T arg, std::memory\_order order = std::memory\_order\_seq\_cst) DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3278             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} myAtomic().fetch\_sub(arg, order);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3279         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3280 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3281         \textcolor{keyword}{operator} T() const DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} load(); \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3282 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3283         T load(std::memory\_order order = std::memory\_order\_seq\_cst) \textcolor{keyword}{const} DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3284             \textcolor{keyword}{auto} result = T();}
\DoxyCodeLine{3285             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(\textcolor{keyword}{auto} \textcolor{keyword}{const}\& c : m\_atomics) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3286                 result += c.atomic.load(order);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3287             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3288             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3289         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3290 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3291         T operator=(T desired) DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{ \textcolor{comment}{// lgtm [cpp/assignment-\/does-\/not-\/return-\/this]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3292             store(desired);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3293             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} desired;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3294         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3295 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3296         \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} store(T desired, std::memory\_order order = std::memory\_order\_seq\_cst) DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3297             \textcolor{comment}{// first value becomes desired"{}, all others become 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3298             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(\textcolor{keyword}{auto}\& c : m\_atomics) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3299                 c.atomic.store(desired, order);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3300                 desired = \{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3301             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3302         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3303 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3304     \textcolor{keyword}{private}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3305         \textcolor{comment}{// Each thread has a different atomic that it operates on. If more than NumLanes threads}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3306         \textcolor{comment}{// use this, some will use the same atomic. So performance will degrade a bit, but still}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3307         \textcolor{comment}{// everything will work.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3308         \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3309         \textcolor{comment}{// The logic here is a bit tricky. The call should be as fast as possible, so that there}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3310         \textcolor{comment}{// is minimal to no overhead in determining the correct atomic for the current thread.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3311         \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3312         \textcolor{comment}{// 1. A global static counter laneCounter counts continuously up.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3313         \textcolor{comment}{// 2. Each successive thread will use modulo operation of that counter so it gets an atomic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3314         \textcolor{comment}{//    assigned in a round-\/robin fashion.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3315         \textcolor{comment}{// 3. This tlsLaneIdx is stored in the thread local data, so it is directly available with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3316         \textcolor{comment}{//    little overhead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3317         std::atomic<T>\& myAtomic() DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{3486             \textcolor{comment}{// NOLINTNEXTLINE(clang-\/analyzer-\/cplusplus.NewDeleteLeaks)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3487             setLast(last -\/ total\_size);}

\DoxyCodeLine{3491             \textcolor{comment}{// copy current data to new location before writing in the union}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3492             memcpy(temp, buf, my\_old\_size); \textcolor{comment}{// skip the +1 ('\(\backslash\)0') for speed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3493             \textcolor{comment}{// update data in union}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3494             setOnHeap();}
\DoxyCodeLine{3495             data.size     = total\_size;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3496             data.capacity = data.size + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3497             data.ptr      = temp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3498             \textcolor{comment}{// transfer the rest of the data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3499             memcpy(data.ptr + my\_old\_size, other.c\_str(), other\_size + 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3500         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3501     \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3502         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(data.capacity > total\_size) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3503             \textcolor{comment}{// append to the current heap block}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3504             data.size = total\_size;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3505             memcpy(data.ptr + my\_old\_size, other.c\_str(), other\_size + 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3506         \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3507             \textcolor{comment}{// resize}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3508             data.capacity *= 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3509             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(data.capacity <= total\_size)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3510                 data.capacity = total\_size + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3511             \textcolor{comment}{// alloc new chunk}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3512             \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* temp = \textcolor{keyword}{new} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}[data.capacity];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3513             \textcolor{comment}{// copy current data to new location before releasing it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3514             memcpy(temp, data.ptr, my\_old\_size); \textcolor{comment}{// skip the +1 ('\(\backslash\)0') for speed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3515             \textcolor{comment}{// release old chunk}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3516             \textcolor{keyword}{delete}[] data.ptr;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3517             \textcolor{comment}{// update the rest of the union members}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3518             data.size = total\_size;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3519             data.ptr  = temp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3520             \textcolor{comment}{// transfer the rest of the data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3521             memcpy(data.ptr + my\_old\_size, other.c\_str(), other\_size + 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3522         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3523     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3524 }

\DoxyCodeLine{3881     \textcolor{comment}{// matching of a string against a wildcard mask (case sensitivity configurable) taken from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3882     \textcolor{comment}{// https://www.codeproject.com/Articles/1088/Wildcard-\/string-\/compare-\/globbing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3883     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} wildcmp(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* wild, \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} caseSensitive) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3884         \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* cp = str;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3885         \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* mp = wild;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3886 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3887         \textcolor{keywordflow}{while}((*str) \&\& (*wild != \textcolor{charliteral}{'*'})) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3888             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}((caseSensitive ? (*wild != *str) : (tolower(*wild) != tolower(*str))) \&\&}
\DoxyCodeLine{3889                (*wild != \textcolor{charliteral}{'?'})) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3890                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3891             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3892             wild++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3893             str++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3894         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3895 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3896         \textcolor{keywordflow}{while}(*str) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3897             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(*wild == \textcolor{charliteral}{'*'}) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3898                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(!*++wild) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3899                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3900                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3901                 mp = wild;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3902                 cp = str + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3903             \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}((caseSensitive ? (*wild == *str) : (tolower(*wild) == tolower(*str))) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{3904                       (*wild == \textcolor{charliteral}{'?'})) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3905                 wild++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3906                 str++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3907             \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3908                 wild = mp;   }
\DoxyCodeLine{3909                 str  = cp++; }
\DoxyCodeLine{3910             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3911         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3912 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3913         \textcolor{keywordflow}{while}(*wild == \textcolor{charliteral}{'*'}) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3914             wild++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3915         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3916         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} !*wild;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3917     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3918 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4273         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}        mib[4];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4274         kinfo\_proc info;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4275         \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t}     size;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4276         \textcolor{comment}{// Initialize the flags so that, if sysctl fails for some bizarre}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4282         mib[1] = KERN\_PROC;}

\DoxyCodeLine{4284         mib[3] = getpid();}

\DoxyCodeLine{4286         size = \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(info);}

\DoxyCodeLine{4290         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4291         \textcolor{comment}{// We're being debugged if the P\_TRACED flag is set.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4386     \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4387     \textcolor{comment}{// There is no 1-\/1 mapping between signals and windows exceptions.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4389     \textcolor{comment}{// but SigInt, SigTerm, etc are handled differently.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4399     \textcolor{keyword}{struct }FatalConditionHandler}

\DoxyCodeLine{4401         \textcolor{keyword}{static} LONG CALLBACK handleException(PEXCEPTION\_POINTERS ExceptionInfo) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4402             \textcolor{comment}{// Multiple threads may enter this filter/handler at once. We want the error message to be printed on the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4403             \textcolor{comment}{// console just once no matter how many threads have crashed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4404             \textcolor{keyword}{static} std::mutex mutex;}

\DoxyCodeLine{4407                 std::lock\_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4408                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(execute) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4409                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} reported = \textcolor{keyword}{false};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4410                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} i = 0; i < DOCTEST\_COUNTOF(signalDefs); ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4411                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(ExceptionInfo-\/>ExceptionRecord-\/>ExceptionCode == signalDefs[i].id) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4412                             reportFatal(signalDefs[i].name);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4413                             reported = \textcolor{keyword}{true};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4414                             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4415                         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4416                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4417                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(reported == \textcolor{keyword}{false})}
\DoxyCodeLine{4418                         reportFatal(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Unhandled SEH exception caught"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4419                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(isDebuggerActive() \&\& !g\_cs-\/>no\_breaks)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4420                         DOCTEST\_BREAK\_INTO\_DEBUGGER();}
\DoxyCodeLine{4421                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4422                 execute = \textcolor{keyword}{false};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4423             \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4430         FatalConditionHandler() \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4431             isSet = \textcolor{keyword}{true};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4432             \textcolor{comment}{// 32k seems enough for doctest to handle stack overflow,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4433             \textcolor{comment}{// but the value was found experimentally, so there is no strong guarantee}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4434             guaranteeSize = 32 * 1024;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4435             \textcolor{comment}{// Register an unhandled exception filter}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4436             previousTop = SetUnhandledExceptionFilter(handleException);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4437             \textcolor{comment}{// Pass in guarantee size to be filled}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4438             SetThreadStackGuarantee(\&guaranteeSize);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4439 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4440             \textcolor{comment}{// On Windows uncaught exceptions from another thread, exceptions from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4441             \textcolor{comment}{// destructors, or calls to std::terminate are not a SEH exception}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4442 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4443             \textcolor{comment}{// The terminal handler gets called when:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4444             \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ std::terminate is called FROM THE TEST RUNNER THREAD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4445             \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ an exception is thrown from a destructor FROM THE TEST RUNNER THREAD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4446             original\_terminate\_handler = std::get\_terminate();}
\DoxyCodeLine{4447             std::set\_terminate([]() DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4448                 reportFatal(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Terminate handler called"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4449                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(isDebuggerActive() \&\& !g\_cs-\/>no\_breaks)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4450                     DOCTEST\_BREAK\_INTO\_DEBUGGER();}
\DoxyCodeLine{4451                 std::exit(EXIT\_FAILURE); \textcolor{comment}{// explicitly exit -\/ otherwise the SIGABRT handler may be called as well}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4452             \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4453 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4454             \textcolor{comment}{// SIGABRT is raised when:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4455             \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ std::terminate is called FROM A DIFFERENT THREAD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4456             \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ an exception is thrown from a destructor FROM A DIFFERENT THREAD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4457             \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ an uncaught exception is thrown FROM A DIFFERENT THREAD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4458             prev\_sigabrt\_handler = std::signal(SIGABRT, [](\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} signal) DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4459                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(signal == SIGABRT) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4460                     reportFatal(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}SIGABRT -\/ Abort (abnormal termination) signal"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4461                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(isDebuggerActive() \&\& !g\_cs-\/>no\_breaks)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4462                         DOCTEST\_BREAK\_INTO\_DEBUGGER();}
\DoxyCodeLine{4463                     std::exit(EXIT\_FAILURE);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4464                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4465             \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4466 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4467             \textcolor{comment}{// The following settings are taken from google test, and more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4468             \textcolor{comment}{// specifically from UnitTest::Run() inside of gtest.cc}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4469 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4470             \textcolor{comment}{// the user does not want to see pop-\/up dialogs about crashes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4471             prev\_error\_mode\_1 = SetErrorMode(SEM\_FAILCRITICALERRORS | SEM\_NOALIGNMENTFAULTEXCEPT |}
\DoxyCodeLine{4472                                              SEM\_NOGPFAULTERRORBOX | SEM\_NOOPENFILEERRORBOX);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4473             \textcolor{comment}{// This forces the abort message to go to stderr in all circumstances.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4474             prev\_error\_mode\_2 = \_set\_error\_mode(\_OUT\_TO\_STDERR);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4475             \textcolor{comment}{// In the debug version, Visual Studio pops up a separate dialog}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4476             \textcolor{comment}{// offering a choice to debug the aborted program -\/ we want to disable that.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4477             prev\_abort\_behavior = \_set\_abort\_behavior(0x0, \_WRITE\_ABORT\_MSG | \_CALL\_REPORTFAULT);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4478             \textcolor{comment}{// In debug mode, the Windows CRT can crash with an assertion over invalid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4479             \textcolor{comment}{// input (e.g. passing an invalid file descriptor). The default handling}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4480             \textcolor{comment}{// for these assertions is to pop up a dialog and wait for user input.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4481             \textcolor{comment}{// Instead ask the CRT to dump such assertions to stderr non-\/interactively.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4482             prev\_report\_mode = \_CrtSetReportMode(\_CRT\_ASSERT, \_CRTDBG\_MODE\_FILE | \_CRTDBG\_MODE\_DEBUG);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4483             prev\_report\_file = \_CrtSetReportFile(\_CRT\_ASSERT, \_CRTDBG\_FILE\_STDERR);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4484         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4485 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4883     \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} trailingBytes(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} c) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4884         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((c \& 0xE0) == 0xC0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4885             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4886         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4887         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((c \& 0xF0) == 0xE0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4888             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4889         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4890         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((c \& 0xF8) == 0xF0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4891             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4892         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4893         DOCTEST\_INTERNAL\_ERROR(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Invalid multibyte utf-\/8 start byte encountered"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4894     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4895 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4896     uint32\_t headerValue(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} c) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4897         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((c \& 0xE0) == 0xC0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4898             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} c \& 0x1F;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4899         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4900         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((c \& 0xF0) == 0xE0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4901             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} c \& 0x0F;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4902         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4903         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((c \& 0xF8) == 0xF0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4904             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} c \& 0x07;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4905         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4906         DOCTEST\_INTERNAL\_ERROR(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Invalid multibyte utf-\/8 start byte encountered"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4907     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4908 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4909     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} hexEscapeChar(\mbox{\hyperlink{classstd_1_1basic__ostream}{std::ostream}}\& os, \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} c) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4910         std::ios\_base::fmtflags f(os.flags());}
\DoxyCodeLine{4911         os << \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)x"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4912             << std::uppercase << std::hex << std::setfill(\textcolor{charliteral}{'0'}) << std::setw(2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4913             << \textcolor{keyword}{static\_cast<}\textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\textcolor{keyword}{>}(c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4914         os.flags(f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4915     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4916 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4919     XmlEncode::XmlEncode( std::string \textcolor{keyword}{const}\& str, ForWhat forWhat )}
\DoxyCodeLine{4920     :   m\_str( str ),}
\DoxyCodeLine{4921         m\_forWhat( forWhat )}
\DoxyCodeLine{4922     \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4923 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4924     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} XmlEncode::encodeTo( \mbox{\hyperlink{classstd_1_1basic__ostream}{std::ostream}}\& os )\textcolor{keyword}{ const }\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4925         \textcolor{comment}{// Apostrophe escaping not necessary if we always use "{} to write attributes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4926         \textcolor{comment}{// (see: https://www.w3.org/TR/xml/\#syntax)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4927 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4928         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}( std::size\_t idx = 0; idx < m\_str.size(); ++ idx ) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4929             uchar c = m\_str[idx];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4930             \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (c) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4931             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'<'}:   os << \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\&lt;"{}}; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4932             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'\&'}:   os << \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\&amp;"{}}; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4933 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4934             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'>'}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4935                 \textcolor{comment}{// See: https://www.w3.org/TR/xml/\#syntax}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4936                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (idx > 2 \&\& m\_str[idx -\/ 1] == \textcolor{charliteral}{']'} \&\& m\_str[idx -\/ 2] == \textcolor{charliteral}{']'})}
\DoxyCodeLine{4937                     os << \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\&gt;"{}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4938                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4939                     os << c;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4940                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4941 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4942             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)"{}'}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4943                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (m\_forWhat == ForAttributes)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4944                     os << \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\&quot;"{}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4945                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4946                     os << c;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4947                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4948 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4949             \textcolor{keywordflow}{default}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4950                 \textcolor{comment}{// Check for control characters and invalid utf-\/8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4951 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4952                 \textcolor{comment}{// Escape control characters in standard ascii}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4953                 \textcolor{comment}{// see https://stackoverflow.com/questions/404107/why-\/are-\/control-\/characters-\/illegal-\/in-\/xml-\/1-\/0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4954                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (c < 0x09 || (c > 0x0D \&\& c < 0x20) || c == 0x7F) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4955                     hexEscapeChar(os, c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4956                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4957                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4958 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4959                 \textcolor{comment}{// Plain ASCII: Write it to stream}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4960                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (c < 0x7F) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4961                     os << c;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4962                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4963                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4964 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4965                 \textcolor{comment}{// UTF-\/8 territory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4966                 \textcolor{comment}{// Check if the encoding is valid and if it is not, hex escape bytes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4967                 \textcolor{comment}{// Important: We do not check the exact decoded values for validity, only the encoding format}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4968                 \textcolor{comment}{// First check that this bytes is a valid lead byte:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4969                 \textcolor{comment}{// This means that it is not encoded as 1111 1XXX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4970                 \textcolor{comment}{// Or as 10XX XXXX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4971                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (c <  0xC0 ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{4972                     c >= 0xF8) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4973                     hexEscapeChar(os, c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4974                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4975                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4976 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4977                 \textcolor{keyword}{auto} encBytes = trailingBytes(c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4978                 \textcolor{comment}{// Are there enough bytes left to avoid accessing out-\/of-\/bounds memory?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4979                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (idx + encBytes -\/ 1 >= m\_str.size()) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4980                     hexEscapeChar(os, c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4981                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4982                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4983                 \textcolor{comment}{// The header is valid, check data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4984                 \textcolor{comment}{// The next encBytes bytes must together be a valid utf-\/8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4985                 \textcolor{comment}{// This means: bitpattern 10XX XXXX and the extracted value is sane (ish)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4986                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} valid = \textcolor{keyword}{true};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4987                 uint32\_t value = headerValue(c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4988                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (std::size\_t n = 1; n < encBytes; ++n) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4989                     uchar nc = m\_str[idx + n];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4990                     valid \&= ((nc \& 0xC0) == 0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4991                     value = (value << 6) | (nc \& 0x3F);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4992                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4993 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4994                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (}
\DoxyCodeLine{4995                     \textcolor{comment}{// Wrong bit pattern of following bytes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4996                     (!valid) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{4997                     \textcolor{comment}{// Overlong encodings}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4998                     (value < 0x80) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{4999                     (                 value < 0x800   \&\& encBytes > 2) || \textcolor{comment}{// removed "{}0x80 <= value \&\&"{} because redundant}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5000                     (0x800 < value \&\& value < 0x10000 \&\& encBytes > 3) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{5001                     \textcolor{comment}{// Encoded value out of range}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5002                     (value >= 0x110000)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5003                     ) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5004                     hexEscapeChar(os, c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5005                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5006                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5007 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5008                 \textcolor{comment}{// If we got here, this is in fact a valid(ish) utf-\/8 sequence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5009                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (std::size\_t n = 0; n < encBytes; ++n) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5010                     os << m\_str[idx + n];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5011                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5012                 idx += encBytes -\/ 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5013                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5014             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5015         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5016     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5017 }

\DoxyCodeLine{5990             \textcolor{keyword}{auto} failwidth = int(std::ceil(log10((std::max(p.numTestCasesFailed, \textcolor{keyword}{static\_cast<}\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned}\textcolor{keyword}{>}(p.numAssertsFailed))) + 1)));}
